Yan Baohang Talks About the Strength and Status of the Volunteer Army 83

The Military Strength is Confirmed to be More Than 300,000, and the Retreat of the Soviet Army Has No Impact

Yan Baohang, a representative of the Northeast People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association and a director of the Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang People's Support Association, came to Shanghai from Peiping a few days ago. The reporter took a special trip to visit him at his residence. He answered in detail about the strength and status of the Northeast Volunteer Army. Now it is urgently disclosed as follows. Since the active activities of the Northeast Volunteer Army this summer, the news here has been extremely dull. The reports from various parties have not been detailed. After all, the Northeast Volunteer Army can be divided into four aspects due to geographical relations: Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe. 1. The Liaoning Volunteer Army, in the green gauze tent, was oppressed by the Japanese enemy. Tang Juwu's 30,000 troops in Liaodong had to temporarily hide and wait for opportunities to act. The 30,000 troops under Deng Tiemei, Li Zirong, and Liu Jingwen are fighting the Japanese enemy in Xiuyan, Zhuanghe, and Fengcheng. They have repeatedly inflicted heavy damage on the enemy. This unit has strong strength, excellent discipline, and rich experience after years of bloody battles. Moreover, the terrain is dangerous, and it is easy to defend and difficult to attack. It can definitely last for a long time. Although the enemy launched a large-scale attack, they suffered losses for more than half a month. The 25,000 troops under Zhu Jiqing, Liu Zhendong, Liu Guitang, Zheng Guilin, etc. in western Liaoning have now been fully replenished and are acting in Suizhong, Xingcheng, Jinxi, and Yixian to contain the enemy. As for the small units of the Volunteer Army lurking in the entire Liaoning Province, there are still 10,000 people. 2. The Jilin Volunteer Army is mainly composed of Ding Chao, Li Shuan, and Wang Delin. Ding and Li's troops have 75,000 people, and Wang Delin's troops have 25,000 people. They are fighting the enemy in more than a dozen counties in eastern Jilin, such as Mishan, Baoqing, Tongjiang, and Dunhua. The Japanese are limited by the dangerous terrain and cannot succeed even if they try to attack. In addition, there are Volunteer Armies under Tian Lin, Fu Dianchen, and Li Futing, numbering no less than 10,000, who are active in the Acheng area and attack Harbin from time to time. The enemy troops are extremely worried. 3. The Heilongjiang Volunteer Army still has 56,000 people, including 20,000 under Deng Wen, more than 10,000 under Li Haiqing, a total of 10,000 under Xu Zihe and Xu Jingde, 4,000 under Pu Bingshan, and 5,000 under Chai Hongyou, all under General Ma. As for Su Bingwen's army, which originally had only 10,000 people, except for the 3,000 people who have retreated into Russia, the 7,000 people under Zhang Dianjiu, the commander of the forward, are still in a certain place in Heilongjiang, contacting the various troops of General Ma, and contacting the enemy from time to time. A certain commissioner of the association went to Heilongjiang twice, totaling eight months. He personally inspected the various armies and witnessed the combat process. He returned recently after the retreat of the Soviet army. According to him, the morale of the various armies is extremely high, and the retreat of the Soviet army has no impact. However, due to insufficient military strength, they urgently need assistance. This is a critical moment for the army, and the people of the country should quickly find ways to help. 4. The Japanese army has been plotting for Rehe for a long time. The people of the province are aware of this and have already organized people's groups to prepare for self-defense. Once something happens, they can fight. The most important thing is to concentrate the 30,000 cavalry under Feng Zhanhai on the border. This unit has been fully replenished and is a strong army. In short, these more than 300,000 strong men have vowed to fight the enemy to the death and will never retreat. The entire people of the Northeast, unable to bear the slaughter and trampling of the Japanese invaders, have unanimously risen up to cooperate with the Volunteer Army to save themselves. They only hope that the whole country will unite as one and actively provide spiritual and material assistance in order to recover the lost land and return our rivers and mountains. This would be very fortunate.

Sun Ke Issues a Statement 84

The Significance of Implementing Constitutional Government and the Understanding That the People Should Have

Sun Ke issued a statement saying that since the founding of the Republic of China, the country has been in danger and the people's livelihood has been in decline, and there has never been a situation as serious as today. The people of the country are sighing and lamenting, sitting in a city of sorrow every day, as if they are waiting to die with their hands tied, and there is nothing they can do. However, they do not know that the national crisis is , and the people's hearts have not died. There are many ways to save the country, and it is already time to do something after . This is why I still have to say a word on this New Year's Day to inform the people of the country and encourage myself. The people of the country have countless expectations for our party comrades after years of ruling, and our party comrades have also worked hard day and night in their work. However, if we examine its effectiveness and calculate its daily strength, it is not only that people have said that there are many dissatisfactions, but even our party comrades, in the quiet of the night, examine themselves and ask themselves, and why are they not panicking and sweating endlessly? The reason for this is nothing more than the lack of sincerity in unity. If we look at the political situation in recent years, the reason why disputes have emerged endlessly is that our party comrades are suspicious of each other, so that the small ones have different ambitions, and the struggle of factions arises from this. The big ones have evolved into the ups and downs of political tides due to conflicts of rights, and wars cannot but continue because of this. Therefore, the doctrine cannot be implemented, the construction cannot be advanced, and the suffering of the people's livelihood has increased. Foreign troubles and internal worries have come one after another. The loss of the three northeastern provinces is only the most prominent of its bad results. Knowing that the source of chaos lies in the lack of sincerity in unity among the people of the country, there is no other way for us to correct the mistakes of the past than to open our hearts to each other in sincerity. This statement may seem like a idealistic theory on the surface, which is not suitable for the circumstances, but if we carefully examine it and prove it with the actual conclusion, we should not treat it as a empty theory. Our country has a population of 400 million, and the number of people is unparalleled in the world, but its strength is not as good as a small country, because it is a plate of loose sand. No matter how large the number is, how can it withstand the ravages of storms without failing? The Kuomintang of China is the only political party in our country with organization, doctrine, and history. However, in recent years, factions have emerged, and forces have been dispersed, resulting in fragmentation and mutual deception. Comrades are too busy killing and excluding each other, so how can they focus their minds and talents on promoting the doctrine? Therefore, the Communists are rampant and cannot be eliminated, and the imperialists are invading and cannot be resisted. There is a reason for this. Therefore, we only hope that the people of the whole country will be able to eliminate the heart of selfishness, then the suspicion will be eliminated, and if the suspicion is eliminated, then the strength of unity can be consolidated. If the strength of unity is consolidated, then the ability to defend oneself will be strengthened, just like a plate of loose sand is mixed with viscous matter, and the strong and firm cement can be established and waited for its completion. Sincerity is like the viscous quality. Without sincerity, the unity is not strong. This is why we focus on sincerity. It is not without purpose.

However, what is described above is abstract. If there is only sincerity, but there is no concrete fact to follow, then the way to save the country is still far away. What is the concrete fact? That is, what kind of system should be adopted to be sufficient to suit the sincere expression of the people of the whole country, and to be sufficient to suit the trend of unity of the people of the whole country, so that the actions of the entire nation can be planned carefully in advance, so that the minds and talents of the people of the whole country can contribute to the survival of the country and the prosperity of the nation. Then the restoration of national fortune can double its speed. In the past, the Prime Minister once stipulated the revolutionary program as three periods: military government, tutelage, and constitutional government. Now the military government period is over, and the tutelage period has also been tried for several years. How effective is it? We will not discuss it in detail for the time being. However, in this current national crisis, when we must concentrate our national strength to save the country, we should adopt the system that is most suitable for concentrating our national strength. I proposed the "Program for Resisting Japan and Saving the Country" this spring, advocating the end of the tutelage in the shortest possible time and preparing for the start of constitutional government. The Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee repeated its meaning this time and proposed the "Concentrating National Strength to Save the Country", also taking the preparation for the start of constitutional government as its premise. It has been passed by the plenary session and can be carried out step by step. Because the party rule in recent years has been affected by political groups, the efficiency is low, the expectations of the people have been deep, and the faith in our party has not been gradually lost, so that the national strength cannot be concentrated, and it cannot resist foreign aggression. This is something that our party comrades did not expect, and it is not a good policy for the current urgent environment. This is why I resolutely promote constitutional government as a remedy. However, while we are preparing for the start of constitutional government, we should also step up the unfinished work during the tutelage period, so that on the one hand, the party rule can come to an end, and on the other hand, the goal of concentrating the strength of the entire nation can be achieved. Internally, we can eliminate the communists, and externally, we can resist the powerful enemies, so as to restore the fate of the Chinese nation and seek the supreme plan for survival.

However, the realization of constitutional government is even more difficult than military government and tutelage. If the people of the country think that once the constitution is formulated, promulgated and implemented, they can easily obtain the good results of constitutional government, it is a big mistake. Because before the national government prepares for the start of constitutional government, the mission of the Kuomintang comrades on the facilities of constitutional government is doubled, and the responsibility of the people of the whole country is also more important than before. The merits of the work during the tutelage period can still be blamed on the Kuomintang, and the merits of constitutional government are the responsibility of the people of the whole country. Therefore, the people must raise their spirits and pay attention to political issues. At the same time, they must fully express their will in a proper manner. On the negative side, they must be able to prevent the old evils in politics, so that the corrupt forces cannot raise their heads. On the positive side, they should urge the government to carry out construction projects to relieve the suffering of the people's livelihood. Then they will not live up to the good name of constitutional government, and the initial intention of promoting and implementing constitutional government. If they repeat the mistakes of the early years of the Republic of China and only provide opportunities for politicians to make trouble, then it is not what we expect from the people. However, if someone holds this to challenge the implementation of constitutional government, then they will fall into the disease of giving up eating because of choking. It is like parents seeing their children stumbling when they are learning to walk, so they forbid them to try again. Then the children will never learn to walk. Is this the attitude that parents should take? Even the most foolish people know that it is impossible. The meaning of promoting constitutional government today is also the same. It must not be said that it should cause stumbles, and it should not be allowed to try again. It all depends on how much we maintain and support.

Shao Yuanchong Discusses the Affairs of the Legislative Yuan 85

Xin Sheng News Agency said that after the recent Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee, there have been various rumors outside about the reorganization of the Legislative Yuan. A few days ago, Shao Yuanchong, the acting president of the Legislative Yuan, came to Shanghai for recuperation. The reporter took a special trip to visit him at his residence yesterday and asked him about the process and his opinions on the future conduct of the Legislative Yuan. According to Shao, I have been acting as the president of the Legislative Yuan twice, and I deeply believe that the responsibility of legislation is related to the rise and fall of the rule of law. Therefore, on the one hand, I promoted the progress of legislative work to build the foundation of the rule of law. At the same time, I also tried my best to recruit academic experts for the committee members and staff to create an academic political institution. Therefore, since I have been acting as the president of the Legislative Yuan twice, I have strived for stability in the institution itself, made progress on the right track, sought progress in the current situation, and created an academic institution. The effects of its facilities have been well received by the general public and the international community. I have also upheld the meaning of "leading and working hard", and I go to the court every day to do my best to be responsible and to promote it. In the past two years, the court meetings have never been interrupted once. I have only been to Shanghai twice, once when the comrades in Guangdong came to Shanghai last winter to meet and talk to promote internal unity, and once in July of this year, when Mr. Yingshi's Memorial Hall was completed, Mr. Chen Aishi telegraphed to attend the meeting and report on Mr. Yingshi's history. That's all. At other times, even when the presidents of the various courts were completely away from Beijing, I still stayed in Beijing to maintain the credibility of the government. This is the past that can be checked. During the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee this time, the Central Committee urged Sun Ke to come and preside over the affairs of the court. I have no prejudice. As for the relationship between Comrade Sun and me, except that during the plenary session, I had to visit the general Central Committee members, so I passed by the Lizhi Society and dropped a name card. There was no contact with Comrade Sun in the Lizhi Society. Only on the morning of the closing of the plenary session, when I went to the Central Party Headquarters, because the meeting had not yet started, I had a three- or four-minute conversation with Comrade Sun in the rest room of the conference hall. I took the meaning of "the old Yin's policy must be told to the new Yin". Regarding the future affairs of the court, I put forward two principles to Comrade Sun: 1. The original members of the Legislative Yuan, except for those who cannot hold concurrent positions due to concurrent positions, should continue as much as possible with the old members who have rich academic qualifications and experience, so that the original legislative work will not be interrupted. Other newly appointed members must be based on the academic qualifications, qualifications, and professional knowledge that the court needs, so that the content can be enriched. For the staff, they should be based on the central government's laws and regulations to protect civil servants, and should be changed less to prevent the affairs from being stopped. Such facts of protecting civil servants have been found in various courts in recent years. For example, after the death of Premier Tan, President Chiang also served as the head of the Executive Yuan, and the original Secretary-General Lu Bichou and other personnel were not changed. After Comrade Ju Juesheng became the President of the Judicial Yuan, the original Secretary-General Xie Guansheng and others were not changed. When the Control Yuan was established, Comrade Chen Guofu served as the acting president of the court and appointed Comrade Yang Pusheng as the Secretary-General. Later, after the President took office, they have not been changed for many years. These are all facts that can be proved. Therefore, what I talked to Comrade Sun at that time was entirely for the sake of maintaining legislative work, so I advocated enriching the candidates for the committee members and changing the internal affairs less. That's all. There is absolutely no intention to ask Comrade Sun to accommodate the list I submitted and the personnel who need to be retained in the candidates or staff, or to have any other conditions. As for Comrade Sun's statement that the list should be submitted in the name of the President of the Court, there are indeed such written regulations in the Organic Law of the National Government. In fact, the political procedure of the Kuomintang is a complex procedure, and in fact, the appointment of political officials must first be decided at the Political Conference, and then the National Government will issue the appointment. This has been a long-standing practice. Therefore, the appointment of the first and second legislative members was jointly submitted by former President Hu and Vice President Lin to the Central Political Council for approval. These are all precedents that can be checked. Therefore, I have no right to abandon this right to jointly propose a motion in the Central Political Council, and the Central Political Council cannot abandon its authority before the power to appoint political officials in the Central Political Council is abolished. As for the rumors that I resigned due to disagreements and that the central government comforted me, etc., they are completely inconsistent with the facts. My departure is always at the command of the central government, and I have no prejudice. When no one is responsible for the affairs of the court, I am acting as the president of the court, and there is nothing to hand over, so how can I give up suddenly? Within a few days, when my illness is slightly better, I should return to Beijing and wait quietly for the central government to decide on a solution. It is not convenient to express any opinions at this time. However, what I am earnestly hoping that the central government and the people of the country will pay attention to at this time is that the foundation of the Republic of China depends on the rise and fall of the rule of law. The ruling party and the people must pay attention to the principles of morality and law, and then politics can be advanced from the normal track. Today, ordinary party members have also advocated shortening the tutelage and starting constitutional government. However, under what conditions can the tutelage be completed? Zhang Junguang Safely Escapes Danger 86

Kidnapped on the 28th, Almost Met With Disaster, Escaped on the 31st, Fortunately Uninjured

The Huadong News Agency reports that Zhang Junguang, Standing Director of the National Joint Association of Salvation Organizations of All Circles, suddenly went missing. He safely escaped danger yesterday morning, the 31st. The news was met with joy. Upon hearing this news, a reporter from the Huadong News Agency immediately went to Zhang's residence in the French Concession to inquire, but the entire family was out. Later, guided by Miss Zhou Shihua, Zhang's fiancée, to a hospital in western Shanghai, they were able to meet with Mr. Zhang and have a half-hour conversation. Mr. Zhang recounted

the kidnapping process in great detail. According to him, around 11:00 AM on the 28th, he went out to meet with Mr. Lin Kanghou at the Bankers' Association. After taking his leave, he took Tram No. 17 on Beijing Road to the intersection of Huajin Lane on Fourth Road. Walking east, he intended to go to the Sino-Western Pharmacy to discuss advertisements for the association's special publication. Unexpectedly, after walking only a few steps, two burly men suddenly appeared with pistols and seized him to take him away. At that time, he knew things were not good, but with pistols pressing tightly against his waist on both sides, he had no ability to resist. He could only follow them, turning into a side road in Maijia Circle, where a car pulled up. He was forced into the car, and black-painted glasses were put on him. The car then drove off, and he could no longer see anything, only hearing the sounds of trams and ships' horns outside the car. After the car had been driving for a long time, he was taken into a house and detained in a room. It was airtight and he did not hear any sounds. In the evening, a woman brought him dinner, but fearing other motives, he did not eat it despite being hungry.

The next afternoon, the two men came again, still with the glasses, and took him into a car. They drove even further, and there was no noise outside the car. After a long time, he was taken into a small boat, his hands were tied behind his back, and he was ordered to lie in the cabin. The boat's hatch was tightly covered, and he had no idea where he was. There were also guards at both ends of the cabin, and he was given food, which was simple and inedible. In the evening, a man suddenly arrived and whispered to the person at the stern of the boat for a long time. The words were not very clear, but it seemed to be: "This is the right person. [對的]" "Tomorrow you can collect the money." Before leaving, he repeatedly urged them to be careful in guarding him.

At noon on the 30th, it was the third day of his kidnapping. Everything was the same as before, with no changes. In the afternoon, another person arrived, and the guard asked if the money had been received. The man replied, "No, I'm afraid we'll have to wait until tomorrow." The guard said, "[Wait 慢], it's not too late to strike after we get the money." After staying for a moment, the man left. At this point, Mr. Zhang knew his life was in danger and was eagerly thinking of a way to escape. However, the guards were strict, making it difficult to slip through. He looked around, but had no good plan. Just as he was anxious, he suddenly saw a small knife inserted on the awning, like the kind used by Jiangbei peddlers to peel water chestnuts. He considered it carefully. At night, the cold air was biting, and he lay in the cabin, shivering and trembling. The guards, due to days of hard work, were very tired and all dozed off. He seized this opportunity and carefully cut the ropes binding his hands behind his back with the knife, little by little. After about two or three hours, he finally freed himself. Just as he was about to crawl out of the cabin, the person guarding the entrance of the boat suddenly went out to urinate and stood at the bow of the boat. At this time, Mr. Zhang did not move, held his breath, tiptoed up behind him, and pushed him hard from behind, causing him to fall into the river. He then

ran ashore in a hurry. He ran wildly in the darkness. The guards seemed to be chasing closely behind him, but fortunately the moonlight was dim, and he finally escaped. After walking for about a few hours, the weather gradually cleared, and he saw railway tracks. After asking the locals several times, he arrived at Jiangwan, where he hired a car to a friend's house and was able to inform his family. At this point, he finally turned danger into safety, fortunately without injury, only feeling extremely tired and in need of rest, he said. Later, Mr. Zhang also

made a statement, saying, "Since the Manchurian Incident, the aggression of Japanese imperialists has become increasingly serious, but they only fear the volunteer armies outside the passes and the national anti-Japanese organizations. Although I dare not determine who instigated this kidnapping, it is very clear that they want to undermine the national salvation movement. This safe return is truly a great blessing in misfortune. From now on, I will continue to work hard to see it through to the end, and I will never be subdued by violence." Furthermore, according to

another report, Mr. Zhang's near-disaster caused anxiety among former Kuomintang elders in Shanghai, such as Zhou Zhenlin, and Central Committee members such as Cheng Qian and Li Liejun, who personally went to inquire. They are overjoyed that he has returned safe and sound. As for Mr. Zhang, due to physical exhaustion, he took a car to Hangzhou that evening to rest.

Otherwise, if all agencies tend to be lax and filled with stagnation, even if there are one or two facilities that are on the right track and agencies with relatively commendable results, they will inevitably become chaotic and degenerate. The comrades in the central government have a common responsibility for the future of politics, which I will not neglect. Now that the country is in crisis and the building is about to collapse, the responsibility for saving the country is shared by the government and the people. But as long as there is someone to take over, I am willing to engage in more arduous work to save the country, and I will never be content with inaction and be a pampered sparrow."

Minutes of the Municipal Council Meeting 88

Two Hundred and Twenty-Fourth Meeting

The 224th Municipal Council Meeting of the Shanghai Municipal Government was attended by Yin Rugeng, Luo Panhui, Wu Xingya (representing Wu Huanru), Wen Hongen, Cai Zengji, Shen Yi, Pan Gongzhan (representing Chen Bai), Li Ting'an, Jin Liren (representing Yang Nianzu), and Xu Peihuang. (A) Reports: The Director of the Finance Bureau reported that: (1) 4.8 million yuan of the Reconstruction Public Bonds had been remitted to the Bureau by Jardine Matheson & Co.; (2) the recent situation of promoting special prize tickets for the International Charity Horse Race. The Director of the Health Bureau reported on the progress of the city's preparations for meat inspection. The Director of the Public Works Bureau reported that he was negotiating with the City Bank to borrow 40,000 yuan for the construction of houses by villagers in Jiangwan Township. (B) Discussions: (1) Regarding the allocation of funds by the Post-War Rehabilitation Preparatory Committee of the Songhu War Zone to dredge the city's rivers. Resolved: The part about collecting land taxes will be handed over to the Finance and Land Bureaus for prompt deliberation and reply. The part about the project will be handed over to the Public Works Bureau for surveying and planning, and reported for review. (2) Regarding the increase in the price of first-class tickets for long-distance city ferry services. Resolved: Passed. (3) Regarding the collection of exhibits for the Chinese government pavilion at the Chicago World's Fair. Resolved: Each bureau and office will send representatives to jointly study what items should be sent by the municipal government. The representative of the Secretariat will be designated as the convener. (4) Regarding the dumping of garbage from the Public Concession in the urban area. Resolved: 1. The annual donation amount will remain at 120,000 yuan. 2. The Finance Bureau will stipulate that the expenditure for improving the garbage dumping facilities in the city will be 100,000 yuan and will be included in next year's budget. (5) Regarding the standards for the establishment of municipal committees in each district. Resolved: To be handed over to Counselors Yin and Luo, together with the directors of the Public Security, Social Affairs, and Land Bureaus, for review. (6) Regarding the planning of a new route to connect to the Zhenru Intermodal Station. Resolved: Passed. It will be announced after obtaining the approval of the Ministry of Railways. (7) Continued discussion on the method of the municipal government donating vehicle licenses on behalf of vehicle owners. Resolved: Passed according to the review opinion. It will be implemented from next year. The meeting adjourned.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Successfully Strives for the Abolition of the Suzhou-Hangzhou Navigation Regulations 89

Native Goods Loaded on Civilian Vessels Exempt From Transshipment Inspection

Inland River Launches in Shanghai, Suzhou, and Hangzhou Exempt From Licensing

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the Jiaxing County Chamber of Commerce, stating that civilian vessels Miao Songrong and Qia Shengxiang were detained by the Jianghai Customs for transporting goods. The Chamber of Commerce argued that civilian vessels transporting goods to the interior had always reported and paid taxes at the Chang Customs and Goods Donation Bureau. Since the national government had clearly ordered the abolition of levies and all Chang Customs and Goods Donation Bureaus had been abolished, there had been no official document stating that civilian vessels transporting goods should report and pay taxes to the customs. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Jianghai Customs requesting prompt release. At the same time, twelve trade associations, including the Shanghai Sugar Industry and North Goods Industry Associations, also jointly sent letters to the Chamber of Commerce, stating that the customs' detention of civilian vessels was inappropriate, and requested the Chamber of Commerce to take charge of the matter. Subsequently, the Customs Commissioner of Jianghai Customs replied to the Chamber of Commerce, stating that the detention of ships and goods was in accordance with the Suzhou-Hangzhou Navigation Regulations, and it was still necessary to pay transshipment tax, etc. However, the previously detained ships and goods of Miao Songrong were released with a warning. After further investigation by the Chamber of Commerce, although Articles 5 to 12 of the regulations contained provisions for civilian vessels to report to customs, register, and pay taxes according to regulations, according to the provisions of Article 1 of the regulations, these civilian vessels referred to steamships towing cargo-laden civilian vessels, not ordinary civilian vessels. Therefore, the title of the regulations was "Regulations on Chinese Steamships Traveling Between Suzhou, Hangzhou, and Shanghai Carrying Passengers and Goods." The title of the regulations could determine the limits of civilian vessels. Moreover, if the customs could collect cargo taxes from civilian vessels, what taxes could levies collect before the abolition of levies? For these reasons, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance three times for clarification and legal correction. On the 30th of this month, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce received Announcement No. 1266 from the Jianghai Customs, which stated: "It is hereby ordered that the 'Regulations for Trial Implementation of Trade Between Chinese and Foreign Steam Launches and Civilian Vessels Traveling Between Suzhou, Hangzhou, and Shanghai,' promulgated in the 22nd year of the Guangxu reign of the former Qing Dynasty, be abolished immediately. Hereafter, the regulations for managing trade at the respective ports shall be handled in the same way as other commercial ports. Native goods loaded on civilian vessels shall be exempt from transshipment tax. However, goods loaded on launches or civilian vessels towed by launches shall be taxed in accordance with ordinary navigation regulations. The issuance of licenses for Chinese and foreign steam launches on the Suzhou and Hangzhou inland waterways shall be discontinued immediately. Launches traveling between Shanghai and Suzhou, Jiaxing, or Hangzhou must still report to customs upon import and export as before." Upon receiving this order, it should be complied with and notified to all shipping merchants for their information. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce has notified the chambers of commerce in Suzhou, Hangzhou, and Shanghai, as well as the various trade associations in Shanghai, of the progress of this matter and the results achieved through persistent efforts.

Pudong Electric Company to Reduce Electricity Prices Starting This Month 90

Pudong Electric Company has been working hard to operate its business in recent years, and its business has become increasingly prosperous. Last year, it was also rated as excellent by the Central Construction Committee and awarded a certificate of honor as encouragement. It is reported that starting this month, the price of electricity for lighting will be reduced to 20 cents per kilowatt-hour. Those who use more electricity will be given discounts according to regulations. The price of electricity will also be appropriately reduced. (1) For those whose average monthly electricity consumption per horsepower is within 150 kilowatt-hours, the price will be reduced to 7 cents per kilowatt-hour. (2) For those whose average monthly electricity consumption per horsepower exceeds 150 kilowatt-hours but is within 250 kilowatt-hours, the price will be reduced to 6.3 cents per kilowatt-hour. (3) For those whose average monthly electricity consumption per horsepower exceeds 250 kilowatt-hours but is within 350 kilowatt-hours, the price will be reduced to 5.6 cents per kilowatt-hour. (4) For those whose average monthly electricity consumption per horsepower exceeds 350 kilowatt-hours, the price will be reduced to 4.6 cents per kilowatt-hour. These prices only apply to users with electric motors installed within 50 horsepower and are the same as the prices in Zhabei. Large users can still receive special discounts. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has approved the record filing and commented that the company has a broad vision and a strong sense of service.

In the Case of Road Construction Beyond the Border, the Japanese Side Insists on Maintaining Police Power in Northern Shanghai 91

Negotiations Have Come to a Standstill

According to the Central News Agency, regarding the negotiations on the recovery of road construction beyond the border, although there has been progress after repeated consultations between the municipal government and the Public Concession's Public Works Department, it has ultimately come to a standstill due to the Japanese director's firm opposition. According to the Japanese side, there is no problem with returning road construction beyond the border to China, but the police power in the area where the Japanese army is stationed in northern Shanghai must always maintain the status quo. The municipal government, being ordered to recover road construction beyond the border, has always insisted on the principle of not losing sovereignty. The Public Works Department, due to the Japanese director's firm attitude, intends to postpone the discussion, so the negotiations on the recovery of road construction beyond the border will be delayed again.

The Chinese Ratepayers' Association Again Requests That Water Use Remain Under the Old System 92

Letter to the Secretary of the Public Works Department

The Chinese Ratepayers' Association yesterday sent a letter to the Secretary of the Public Works Department, stating: "Sir, according to a letter from the Hequn Business Co., Ltd., the British-owned Shanghai Waterworks Company is forcing them to install water meters, otherwise they will threaten to cut off the water. The suffering of the owner should be known to your association. Now, the oppression suffered by our company from the water company is listed below. Our company built 31 shops, No. Yuanyi Lane, at the intersection of Yangshupu Road and Grant Road last spring. When they were completed in June, it was the time when the water company changed to using water meters. It was impossible to achieve the purpose of inclusive water, so we reluctantly installed them. The monthly income from rent there is only 600 yuan, but the water bill is as high as more than 120 yuan, which is already difficult to bear. Unexpectedly, in July of this year, the water bill suddenly increased to 265 yuan, more than double the previous fee. We sent a letter to the water company on August 20 to inquire about the reason for the sudden increase in the water bill. We received their reply on September 5, stating that the water pipes in the two houses, No. 2453 and No. 19 in the lane, were leaking, and that 228 gallons of water were leaking per hour, totaling 164,000 gallons of water leaking per month. Our company immediately sent a letter inviting the Hanxing Company, which originally installed the water pipes, to order craftsmen to repair them. After a detailed inspection by the craftsmen, there was no leakage in any house. At the same time, we also received the water company's August water bill for 239 yuan and 75 cents, which was the same as the previous month. Therefore, on September 20, we sent another letter to the company to question them. We then received a reply on September 24, stating that the water pipes in the two houses, No. 2469 and No. 8 in the lane, were leaking. Our company again invited the Hanxing Company to conduct a second investigation, but there were still no flaws. Of course, we suspected this. On September 30, we sent another letter to the water company to negotiate, stating that the water pipes installed by our company had been used after being inspected and qualified by the water company. How did this leakage occur, and what guarantee is there for the future leakage solution, and should the company be responsible for investigating leakage and repairing water pipes? Now that the meter system has been changed, it is not accurate to charge water fees, so that both parties have no loss, but it must not be changed. The company should have the obligation to investigate leakage, so how can users without experience in water supply engineering be required to bear the accidental losses caused by the company's management and negligence? At the same time, we also stated that the water used in the summer as reported can be calculated at a discount and should be treated the same way, and we hoped for a detailed reply. On the same day, we received a reply stating that inspecting water pipes is not the company's obligation, but in order to reduce our company's burden, after inspection, there were no errors and the rest of the questions were not answered. Later, we repeatedly sent people to negotiate verbally, and the company initially agreed to reduce the water bills for July and August, totaling 505 yuan, 38 cents, to 350 yuan. However, our company was willing to pay according to the water bills paid in the previous twelve months, calculating a total of 121 yuan, 7 cents per month, but the company did not approve it, so it has been delayed until now and has not been resolved. On the 6th of this month, another notice came, limiting the time to before the 13th of this month. If the water bills for two months are not paid in full, the water will be cut off. Our company then reluctantly paid 300 yuan for the water bill on the 20th of this month, which is about 25% more than the monthly fee, but the company actually sent a letter to return the money the next day, saying that it must reach 350 yuan, etc. Our company really can't bear it anymore. Since it concerns the interests of the public, we would rather have the water cut off than be the culprit of setting a precedent. Therefore, we send a special letter requesting that you grant a pointer and provide assistance. This is really a prayer," etc. It has come to the meeting. According to the current method of calculating water fees by meter, the purpose of preventing waste has not been achieved, and the fact that water fees have increased has been seen. Your bureau should quickly order the water company to temporarily maintain the old system before there is a proper way to prevent waste, so as to avoid the actual difficulties in handling the matter.

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers' Association yesterday sent a letter to the Secretary of the Public Works Department, stating, "Sir, according to a letter from ratepayer Lu Wenzhong, our telephone number 52845 has been subject to a price increase by the Shanghai Telephone Company. The Shanghai Telephone Company's only excuse for this price increase is that it has been approved by the Public Works Department. It is natural that the price increase of a public utility company must be approved by the Public Works Department, but the company's main body of operation is tens of thousands of telephone users, and it should also consult with the users on whether they can afford it and go through the formalities of signing a new price contract before it can be done properly. If it relies on the words "approved" to raise the price and "retroactively," I don't know what country's laws this huge company is using. If it can take whatever it wants, then if the Public Works Department approves the company to raise the price retroactively to the beginning of its operation, or even stipulates an increase of one or two hundred taels of silver, will it also force users to submit? After our Chinese users unanimously opposed the price increase, the company repeatedly sent people to lobby and probe, while on the one hand using the means of cutting lines as a threat. We are concerned that once this bad precedent is set, other public utilities will follow suit in the future, and there will be no end to the exploitation of citizens. Therefore, we send a special letter to you, hoping that your association will lead users to fight for their rights." Therefore, we sent a letter to your bureau to promptly take into account the interests of both parties and reconsider the solution.

Pudong Fellow Townsmen Fight for the Municipal Ferry Price Increase 95

The Highest Ferry Price to Pudong is One Yuan, Members' Meeting Will Reconsider

The original ferry services to places such as Gaoqiao, Shanghai, were taken over and operated by the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities long ago. When the fares were increased starting in January of the 21st year, members of the Pudong Fellow Townsmen Association believed that the city government was competing with the people for profit, so they submitted a proposal to the first members' meeting of the Pudong Fellow Townsmen Association for discussion. At that time, it was decided to petition the municipal government to cancel the price increase and design their own ferry service to benefit the common people. Later, due to the outbreak of the January 28th Incident, the rescue efforts were delayed. It is now heard that the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has stated that the ferry service lost 40,000 to 50,000 yuan this year and has petitioned the municipal government to increase fares again starting in January of the 22nd year. The highest fare has been increased to one yuan, and the next year it will be five jiao, which is a world apart from the original fare of only one jiao or a few fen before the municipal government took over the operation. The members of the association, based on the above reasons, have prepared a written opinion and continued to petition the Pudong Fellow Townsmen Association, advocating fairness and pleading for the people. It is reported that the Pudong Fellow Townsmen Association has handed over this petition to the previously organized Ferry Special Committee for discussion and will submit it to the second members' meeting on January 8 of the 22nd year for reconsideration. Because the previous efforts were unsuccessful and the fares have increased again, they will strive to achieve the goal of canceling the price increase.

New Year's Eve Morning: Bullets Flew Like Rain on Tiantong Road 97

Longsheng Rice Shop Robbed in Sudden Raid Early Morning

Manager Zhang Guiqing Shot While Shouting for Help - Critically Injured

Vegetable Vendor Old Woman Killed Instantly by Stray Bullet

Detectives Bravely Pursue, Arresting Many Robbers One After Another

Longsheng Rice Shop, located at 244 to 248 Tiantong Road, Hongkou, is managed by Zhang Guiqing, a native of Zhenhai, 45 years old. At around 7:00 AM yesterday morning, just as the shop was opening its doors, eight robbers suddenly leaped in. All spoke with a Jiangbei accent. Five robbers carried handguns. After entering, the robbers saw the shop assistants and old accountant were still washing up. Taking advantage of their unpreparedness, they ordered them to gather in a corner and herded them into the rice milling warehouse, assigning one robber to guard them with a gun. The rest swarmed upstairs, directly into Zhang's bedroom on the third floor. Zhang was just getting up. Upon seeing the situation, he tried to escape, but it was too late. He was surrounded by the robbers, who demanded he hand over the keys to the safe. Zhang had no choice. The safe was opened and robbed of 500 silver dollars, 1900 paper dollars, and 1100 silver jiao (dimes). Seeing their objective achieved, the robbers rushed downstairs to escape. Zhang immediately followed, and as the robbers exited the front door, he shouted loudly, "Robbers!" At that moment, the robber guarding the rice milling warehouse was still inside. Hearing Zhang's shouts, he rushed out in a panic. Seeing Zhang still shouting, and hearing the police whistle blowing from upstairs, the robber, in desperation, ran out the front door and fired a shot at Zhang, hitting him in the chest. Zhang fell to the ground, bleeding. At that moment, nearby Chinese Constables 2992 and 3063 also heard the alarm and rushed to the scene. Seeing the robbers trying to escape, they stepped forward to apprehend them. The robbers, finding their escape route blocked, opened fire. The constables returned fire, and a fierce gunfight ensued. One of the robbers, Zhu Guangyi, was shot down and captured first. Seeing this, the remaining robbers fled in all directions. However, the Hongkou district police stations had already received the news and dispatched officers to search and capture them. Three more were apprehended. During the gunfight between the detectives and the robbers, bullets flew like rain. A vegetable vendor, the old woman Chen Li, 54 years old, happened to be passing by and was struck in a vital spot by a stray bullet, falling to the ground and dying instantly. Her body was taken to the morgue by police wagon to await examination. Zhang Guiqing and the wounded robber Zhu Guangyi were taken to Tongren Hospital. Zhang's chest wound was severe, and his life was in danger. The wounded robber was shot three times: once in each leg and once in the chest. The three robbers captured were taken to the police station under guard. Under strict interrogation, they identified themselves as Zhu Changmin, 30 years old; Huang Chuanliu Zi, 28 years old; and Liu Chunming, 38 years old, all from Jiangbei. Two handguns and several bullets were recovered. By noon, Hongkou Police Detective Wang Debiao and Detectives Bai Mingfu and Gu Changzhi had apprehended six more accomplices and recovered the stolen goods, all of whom were taken to the police station for detention.

○ ○ ○ ○

Ancient Painting from Jing'an Temple Helps Finance the Military 98

The ancient Jing'an Temple in Western Shanghai has a long history and a rich collection. Unfortunately, it was occupied by itinerant monks, and many treasures were scattered and lost. Only twelve eight-foot-long silk scroll paintings of portraits of virtuous monks from the Yuan Dynasty remain. The craftsmanship is exquisite, and the colors are magnificent. It is said that they were precious items from the Qing imperial palace, specially bestowed upon the temple's famous abbot, the Venerable Zheng Sheng. Zheng Sheng cherished these paintings as if they were priceless jewels. He would only occasionally hang them during major Buddhist festivals. Retired officials and celebrities in Shanghai who saw them were full of praise. The famous contemporary painter Mr. Wang Dun'gen added an inscription of extreme admiration. The value is unimaginable. The current abbot, Zhifa, is young and handsome and has a charitable disposition. He is particularly enthusiastic about patriotic and public welfare causes. Recently, seeing the Northeast Volunteer Army sacrificing their lives for the country, he was filled with admiration and sadness, regretting that he did not have more money to donate to the military. He decided to send these ancestral treasures to the New World Relief Association for Northeast Refugees Art Exhibition for public display, hoping that benevolent gentlemen would purchase them at a high price. He would then entrust all the proceeds to the association to be remitted to the three northeastern provinces to purchase food and military supplies. He hopes that collectors at home and abroad will be inspired to contribute their treasures, generously parting with them for sale, so that a large sum of money can be raised to provide the greatest possible assistance to the Northeast Volunteer Army. If this happens, Zhifa's grand wish will not be in vain.

Zhu Suixuan, Who Impersonated a Department Head of the China Merchants Bureau, Sentenced 99

Admitted to Fraud Without Denial - Sentenced to One Year of Imprisonment

Zhu Suixuan, a native of Yancheng, impersonated a member of the Executive Committee and Chief of the General Affairs Department of the Central China Merchants Bureau. He falsely set up a China Merchants Bureau company office in the pavilion room on the upper floor of 674 East Yalu Road. Under the pretext of introducing inspectors and dockworkers, he defrauded more than 20 fellow villagers, including Wang Yuejiang and Yin Zhaofeng, of several hundred yuan in "movement expenses". After the case was exposed, he was arrested by Chinese Detective Xu Yongyuan and brought before the First Special District Local Court. The details of his interrogation have already been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingkun held a continued hearing in the third criminal court. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer from the police station, stated that during the adjournment, it was discovered that Sun Yujie, Sun Yixuan, Zhang Lanting, Zhang Jinfa, Xiang Xiyuan, Cai Jie, Feng Yulin, and Li Jingyun, all defrauded on the pretext of introducing positions like inspectors, clerks, and workers, were swindled out of more than seventy yuan. They were present in court to testify. Based on the reports of the victims about being defrauded, the defendant admitted without denial after questioning. Judge Xu, after verifying the confession, announced the verdict in court: the defendant was sentenced to one year of imprisonment, and the confiscated name cards and notices were also confiscated.

Borrowed Money Using Fictitious Person's Name 100

Collateral Insufficient to Cover the Debt - Guarantors Also Sued

Lu Yiru, who previously worked as a translator at the former Mixed Court, in July of last year, persuaded his friend Wang Hongyuan to mortgage a large sum of money to the British firm Lianfu Real Estate Company, claiming that the paint was produced in Germany and worth 60,000 to 70,000 taels of silver. The manager of the company, a Briton named Wei Qu, saw the invoices and deeply believed him. He agreed to a mortgage of 25,000 taels of silver and signed a mortgage agreement with a deadline for redemption. However, Lu did not appear in person, but fabricated the name Wang Bofan as the mortgagor, with Sun Youqi, Sun Guozhang, the owner of a certain rice shop, and Wang Hongyuan as guarantors. The contract stipulated that the guarantors' rice shop could not close down before the mortgage was repaid. However, when the deadline arrived, the company repeatedly urged the guarantors to redeem the mortgage, but they ignored it. They then negotiated with Wang Hongyuan, who finally revealed the inside story, stating that it was entirely Lu Yiru who had initiated the matter. Wang Bofan did not exist, and the mortgaged money had been divided and used by them. They were truly unable to redeem the mortgage. The company estimated the value of the collateral to dispose of it. Unexpectedly, the estimated value was less than one-fifth of the mortgage amount. They realized they had been scammed, but still hoped to hold the guarantors accountable. When they saw that the rice shop opened by the two Suns was also empty, they hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit against Lu Yiru and the other three for conspiracy to defraud. Lu desperately begged someone to intercede, hoping to resolve the matter out of court, but no settlement has been reached to this day. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhang Junqing opened the court to summon and examine the defendants. Only Wang Hongyuan appeared in court. Lu Yiru sent lawyer Ye Shaoying to court to request an adjournment to continue trying to settle out of court. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that the defendant's so-called settlement was merely a delaying tactic, and that although the rice shop of the two guarantors had not closed, it was completely empty, posing a risk of them absconding. He requested rapid relief. Judge Zhang stated that because most of the defendants were absent, the hearing could not proceed. He only briefly questioned the plaintiff Wei Qu and the defendant Wang Hongyuan about the mortgage situation and instructed Wu to reschedule the hearing.

Ningbo Native Association Cables Request for Investigation of the Old Ningbo Shatien Sub-Bureau 101

The Ningbo Native Association in Shanghai received a letter yesterday from the Fifth District Office of Yin County, stating that the Old Ningbo Shatien Sub-Bureau had arbitrarily sold the river channels in the Baisha Township area to Qia Ji for management, hindering water conservancy and causing panic among the people. They specially telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Government to swiftly order a halt and to dismiss and investigate Wang Weicheng, the director of the Sub-Bureau, to appease public anger. The original telegram is recorded below: "To the Honored Zhejiang Provincial Government in Hangzhou: The case is based on a letter from the Fifth District Office of Yin County, stating that on the 24th of this month, they received a letter from the Deputy Township Chief Dong Xinkuan of Baisha Township, stating that the public river channels in our township are used by sailing vessels and also serve as a source of water for the residents, which is of great importance to their livelihood, and they have been dredged repeatedly over the years. However, residents along the river recently reported that the river channels along the coast, from Baisha Liangting in the east to Lianfu Temple (i.e., Zhongliangting) in the west, have been secretly sold by the Old Ningbo Shatien Sub-Bureau. Upon hearing this, we were filled with doubt and alarm. After investigation, we observed bamboo sticks inserted on both sides of the riverbank, marked with the words "Qia Ji Boundary," which confirmed the above report. According to the County Government's clear order, the sandy land along the coast of this county, which is related to water conservancy, has long been prohibited from being auctioned off. However, the Shatien Bureau acted wilfully and actually sold the public river channels privately. This not only deprives tens of thousands of residents of water but also endangers the fire safety of the entire township, which is a matter of even greater concern. Our township is located in a remote area and has been repeatedly harassed by the Sub-Bureau. The ignorant villagers obey the orders meticulously. As a result, the sandy fields along the coast that have been forcibly bought by the Bureau are numerous. Now, disregarding the lives and deaths of the people, the public is panicking and does not know what the future holds. Therefore, we respectfully request your office to submit a petition to the County Government, requesting them to negotiate with the Sub-Bureau as soon as possible and issue a notice to reassure the people and emphasize water conservancy. The matter was submitted by the Fifth District Office with a resolution from the 18th District Affairs Meeting to be forwarded to the County Government, and a letter was sent to the Ningbo Native Association in Shanghai, etc., requesting support. After investigation, we found that the Old Ningbo Shatien Sub-Bureau violated the regulations set by the Ministry, illegally auctioned off the privately owned base lands, causing resentment in the villages. Now, they have arbitrarily disposed of the public river channels related to water conservancy, which is extremely illegal. Based on the information in the letter, we urgently request that your office review and approve it, swiftly order a halt, and dismiss and investigate the director of the Sub-Bureau to appease public anger and align with public opinion."

Charity Race Tickets Can Still Be Purchased During the New Year Holiday 107

It is heard that about 80% of the Universal Charity Race Lottery tickets have been sold, and there are not many remaining tickets. Because some of them had not been printed, the ticket offices were temporarily out of stock, and many could not continue to sell them. The situation of resale is generally visible. According to the Finance Bureau, all of the lottery tickets have now been printed and the required numbers have been sent to the various ticket offices yesterday in order to continue sales. However, many companies, banks, and groups in the city will be on New Year's holiday on the 1st, 2nd, and 3rd of the new year, and there is deep concern that ticket buyers will have no way to find out where to buy them. A mutual agreement was obtained from the Shanghai Race Club, that the club will open its doors to sell tickets on the 2nd and 3rd, but only from 10:00 am to 12:00 pm. The bureau will also assign staff to the bureau at the above times to discuss ticket purchases. The reporter also learned yesterday that many people from other places have remitted money to Shanghai to purchase the tickets from the Xinmin and Shenbao newspapers or the Municipal Finance Bureau. It is heard that only the postage fee for registered mail needs to be remitted along with the money, and the tickets can be sent, which is very convenient. Further investigation of various ticket offices such as the Xinxin and Lihua companies shows that the tickets have already been sold out, indicating the enthusiasm of ticket buyers this time. According to those familiar with horse racing, every time the number of champagne tickets is purchased to 80,000 or 90,000, because demand exceeds supply, the market price will rise by one or two yuan. This charity ticket should also have the same situation.

Local Court Burns Narcotics 108

The Shanghai Local Court seized a total of 4,218 pieces of opium, red pills, and smoking paraphernalia from July to the end of September of the 21st year, and most of them were huge pieces. Therefore, the Jiangsu High Court Procuratorate approved the destruction at the end of the 21st year. At 2:00 pm at the end of the year, the representatives of various agencies who attended were Yu Zongchen of the High Procuratorate, Zhang Dabing of the High Second Branch, Ju Zhijing of the First Special Court, Jin Yu of the Garrison Headquarters, Ma Mingzu of the Municipal Government, Shi Keyou of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and Lu Youchang of the Customs. The president of the court, Shen Xiqing, chief prosecutor Lou Ying, prosecutor Zhang Zonghua, etc., invited them to the open courtyard in front of the detention center. The clerks then enumerated the confiscated narcotics one by one, unpacked them for inspection, and then ordered police chief Chen Junfang, police officers Chen Xihui, Zhu Wenqing, etc. to supervise the police to pile the narcotics with pine firewood, lime, kerosene, and salt to burn them. It was not completed until dusk. The remaining ashes were loaded into burlap sacks and sunk in the Pu River to remove the toxic atmosphere.

Hongkou Bank of China Moves Back to New Building 109

Magnificent Architecture... Business Progress

This Month on the 4th... Move into Office

The Hongkou Branch of the Bank of China (referred to as the Hongkou Bank of China) has been open since May of the Republic of China, and has been open for more than three years. The business has made considerable progress. The old building was not enough to apply, so two years ago, I purchased two acres of land at the corner of North Sichuan Road and Haining Road to build a seven-story building, named ［Hongkou China Bank Archives］. The building was designed by Lu Qian of the Bank's Construction Industry. Affected by Shanghai, the project was not without delay. The lowest level has been completed first, and it is scheduled to move back to work on January 4. Its architecture is extremely magnificent, and the style is the latest style. The interior architecture is all marble, and the latest European and American vaults and night vaults are used. In terms of lending, more importance is attached to domestic goods industry and commerce, which is especially unique. The number of domestic goods factories in contact with the bank is not small, and the future development can be predicted.

Flower Lottery Harms People 110

Liu Yuekun from Yangzhou, 23 years old, lives in Maoyeli, Lannidu, Pudong. He is currently working as a tea server in a silver company. Recently, he was obsessed with the flower lottery, thinking of it as a way to get rich, but he lost repeatedly and continuously lost money, which was quite a lot, resulting in a high debt and embarrassment. At around 10:00 pm the night before last, Liu suddenly had a fantasy and secretly went to a broken coffin and took out a skull, moved it to the field at the east end of Pudong Avenue, burned incense and begged, hoping that the ghost would indicate the flower path, in preparation for returning to the capital in case of emergency. His ignorant actions were quite ridiculous. It happened that Luo Hanxin and others, members of the second team of the Security Corps, were patrolling and passed by. They took Liu and the skull back to the team and sent them to the Third District Public Security Bureau. After the district chief questioned him, he ordered the skull to be buried first, and Liu was sent to the General Bureau for disposition.

Also at around 8:00 pm that night, Liu Huansheng, a patrol officer from the Third District, cracked a flower lottery listening device in a thatched house at No. 18 Dongchang Road, and arrested the device owner, Ma Liansheng from Taizhou, and suspects Wang Jianye, Ding Weiyu, and three others, along with a bunch of flower lottery paper slips, three flower lottery folds, a flower lottery book, three flower lottery charts, a bunch of blank charts, and gambling money of six yuan. They were taken to the district together. The district chief sentenced Wang and Ding to three days of detention for improper behavior, and the device owner was sent to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Senior Anhui Jiang Resident Huang Zhiqiong Passes Away 111

Huang Zhiqiong, a senior resident of Anhui Jiang, had a vast knowledge and many writings. Those that have been published include Huang Zi's Twenty Articles and Poems on History, which have been circulated throughout the country. In his youth, he was appreciated by Li Wenzhong and participated in the secretariat. He was also hired as the chief Chinese instructor at the Beiyang Military Academy. Beiyang seniors Wang Shizhen, Duan Qirui, Feng Guozhang, etc. were all his students. He held official positions in Jiangsu and Zhejiang for a long time, serving as supervisor. He was later transferred to the Chief Commander of the Changmen Fortress in Fujian and the Chief of the Anhui Finance Department, and served as a political councilor. He was well-known wherever he went, and founded the Minhou Fortress Artillery Special School and the Anhui Military Academy. Many of his students were outstanding figures of the time, such as the martyrs Chen Gengxin and Feng Chaoji, who died in Huanghuagang, and their contributions are still fresh in people's minds. There are even more who participated in the National Revolution. Mr. Huang always gave generously to help others and did not care about family property. In his later years, he lived in Shanghai, entertaining himself with poetry and calligraphy, talking about ancient and modern events. He was energetic and happy, and never seemed tired. He was seventy-four years old. He died peacefully at Mao time on December 28, 21st year. At the time of his death, he was clear-minded. After his death, his sons, Bodu, Zhongsu, and Pishen, personally helped the body to the Chinese Funeral Home on Haige Road. On the 29th, the guests who came to pay their condolences included Xu Jingren, Wang Yiting, Wu Tie, Wang Zhengting, Ye Gongzhuo, Wen Lanting, Li Zuzhuo, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Zheng Hongnian, Huang Hanzhi, Wang Peiyuan, Chen Yuanshi, Zhao Jinqing, Yu Jingping, Fan Yichu, Zhu Qiluo, Sun Faxu, Li Cishan, and hundreds of leaders from all walks of life. Plain cars and white horses, extremely mournful.

Male Corpse Hangs Himself on Tree 112

Late the night before last, an unnamed man, about thirty years old, wearing a blue cloth shirt and foreign trousers, for unknown reasons, went to a large tree in the open space at the northwest corner of the intersection of Qiqi Road and West Ais Road in the French Concession and hanged himself with hemp rope. At 5:00 am yesterday, a patrol officer passed by and reported to the police station. Detectives were sent to remove the body. Seven pawn tickets were found on his body, but nothing else. The body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch to examine the body. No family members were found. At 10:00 am, the Second Special District Court was notified and commissioned Prosecutor Deng Baosun to come to the place and examine the body. It was confirmed that the deceased had hanged himself to death. The corpse was ordered by Tongren Fuyuan Hall to be buried according to the regulations. The seven pawn tickets were stored in the warehouse for collection.

Rice Shop Employee Robbed While Collecting Debts 113

More than Four Hundred Yuan Robbed

Jiang Xu, a partner in Hongchang Rice Shop in Nan Shi Fengji Wharf, yesterday was the date for closing accounts for the New Year's Eve, so the shop sent Jiang to Xie Da Rice Shop in Shenyi Fang, Datong Road, Zhabei at about 2:40 pm to collect accounts. Jiang took a chartered car and went there. A total of four hundred seventy-seven yuan one jiao two fen were collected. When he was returning to the intersection of Datong Road and Taiyang Temple Road, four robbers suddenly came from the roadside, three wearing blue cloth shirts and pants, and one wearing black cloth shirts and pants, all speaking with a local accent. They shouted for the coachman to stop. Three robbers blocked the chartered car. Jiang's coachman knew that something was wrong and tried to escape from the side, but was still blocked and slapped twice. Another robber then took out a handgun to warn him not to make a sound. Jiang and the coachman were then left to do as they were told. The four hundred seventy-seven yuan one jiao two fen on Jiang's body was all robbed. The three robbers then fled to the south, and one robber still used a gun to order the coachman to drag Jiang Xu to the north. Jiang knew that it was difficult to resist, so he ordered the coachman to run to the nearby Fourth District Police Station to report. The police station immediately reported to the General Office to send police to pursue the robbers and ordered the detective team to investigate the case in secret.

Reader Advisory

(1) How Should [Production Rationalization] Be Interpreted? 122

丨Letter from Mr. Shen Yimin丨

In the [Reader Advisory] column of your newspaper on December 27th, in the letter published by Mr. Zhu Ying, there is a sentence I am somewhat skeptical about. He said: [...... Even if you find work, it is either the factory closing due to the influence of the current situation, or the result of production rationalization that leaves you exhausted all day without being able to eat your fill.] According to Mr. Zhu's meaning, production rationalization is the root cause of his [being exhausted all day without being able to eat his fill]. In fact, this is not the case. We know that the content of production rationalization is nothing more than: (1) organizing the factory with extremely scientific methods, simplifying the relationship between departments, and saving as much as possible in terms of materials and time, or producing more products in the same amount of time and with the same amount of materials; (2) making every effort to innovate machinery so that the products that formerly required the labor of ten or hundreds of people can now be produced with the labor of only one or ten people; (3) universally electrifying factories, so that machines that formerly required ten or hundreds of people to manage now only require one or ten people; (4) transportation and traffic are all under the control of electrification and mechanization, so that the transportation of products and materials is extraordinarily rapid and saves a great deal of labor and time. Rationalization itself is not sinful; the sin lies in the private system of production for the sake of commodities. Implementing production rationalization in a private production society, its purpose is only to increase the production of commodities; to intensify the exploitation of labor; to save production methods as much as possible; and to dissolve accumulated capital as much as possible. The result is only overproduction, factory closures, which forms the so-called [population surplus] and worker unemployment. However, this does not mean that production rationalization will have this phenomenon as soon as it is implemented in the current society, but rather that when it develops to a certain extent, it will inevitably lead to a greater economic panic. We can understand this by looking at the results of production rationalization in the United States and Germany. However, we can draw an opposite conclusion from production rationalization in the existing private production society, which is: in a higher, new social relationship of production, this kind of production rationalization is 100% necessary, and it is a necessary condition; therefore, the first necessary condition for production rationalization at a higher level is: shortening working hours. Why shorten working hours? In order to increase the cultural level of workers, so that they can spend most of their time enjoying spiritual happiness and higher education, because in this society, production is no longer for the production of commodities, but for the consumption of the producers themselves; the planned economy of the Soviet Union also reveals this clue. I am afraid that Mr. Zhu, because he curses the production rationalization of the current society and also hates and opposes the production rationalization of the rational society of the future, would be greatly dangerous. I would like to ask Mr. Zhu with a word and ask your reporter for advice. Is there any merit in this? I hope you can enlighten me.

Reply: Your letter expresses the essence of production rationalization with great insight, which can greatly supplement what Mr. Zhu has not expressed. Mr. Zhu is suffering from illness and deeply affected by the exploitation of the capitalists. He is feeling sentimental for a moment, [illegible] calm and precise analysis. Mr. Zhu should also agree with what you said. However, I would like to add one point here, which is that production rationalization is the highest manifestation of the production method of a commodity production society, but this highest production method becomes incompatible with the production relations from which it came to a certain extent. As a result, it digs a grave for the social organization formed by this production relationship. [Please come in], and breaks out of its womb, becoming the [darling] of a higher stage of social organization. What do you think of this high-level insight?

(2) The [Starvation] Problem 123

丨Letter from Mr. Sun Jingren丨

Your reporter said in response to Mr. [Blank]'s reply on the 19th of this month: [As long as you endure hardship, you will never starve to death.] I am somewhat skeptical about this statement. If we are to encourage people to work hard and not sit idle and eat, then saying this may have a one-sided reason, and the good intentions of the speaker can be reasonably excused. However, in the current society, this statement is really not enough to be a lesson, because most of the people who have already starved to death, or are about to starve to death, or will inevitably starve to death in the future, are willing to [endure hardship] and really endure hardship], while those who live in luxury, ride tall horses and drive fancy cars, and indulge in extravagance and dissipation are mostly people who cannot endure hardship, are unwilling to endure hardship, and specialize in using the [hardship] of others to supply his sacrifices. Take me as an example. From morning to night, I work more than twelve hours in the store, both managing the accounts for the owner and running errands for him; both wiping the tables and sweeping the floor, and doing business for him. Except for eating and sleeping, there is not a moment of free time all day long. However, I only earn twenty yuan a month, and apart from my food, clothing, and shelter, there is nothing left to support my mother. If I want to support my mother, I have to go hungry. But I am still lucky to have twenty yuan a month. There are hundreds of thousands of others in Shanghai who are willing to endure hardship and are able to endure hardship, but cannot find work anywhere. Since they have no work, the daring ones have to become thieves and kidnappers, and the weak ones have to commit suicide by throwing themselves into the Huangpu River. So, I think this way: those who starve to death are not necessarily people who are unwilling to endure hardship or unable to endure hardship; and those who do not starve to death are not necessarily all people who are willing to endure hardship or able to endure hardship. Quite the contrary. And further observation: the current society is, on the one hand, making every effort to create [hardship] for people, and on the other hand, making every effort to create opportunities for people to be unwilling to endure hardship and [live in ease and comfort]. Is this correct? I humbly ask for your clear understanding.

Reporter's Note: Regarding our reply to Mr. Weng's question about economic difficulties [annual income of more than 200 yuan, a family of six or seven, debts of more than 3,000 yuan, and the end of the year is approaching, how to cope?] (Mr. Weng's original letter and our reply can be found in this column on the 19th of this month), we have received two letters from Mr. Zhu Ying before and after, having detailed discussions with us. (See this column on the 22nd and 27th) Mr. Zhu's intention is that we should not vaguely tell Mr. Weng that this is a whole social problem, but simply vaguely call him to [endure hardship]. Regarding this point, we have already explained it in our two replies to Mr. Zhu, that is, we have already explained in our reply to Mr. Weng that this is a whole social problem, but the wording is slightly vague. Now we have received another letter from Mr. Sun, continuing to correct our words about calling Mr. Weng to [endure hardship]. Although Mr. Sun's opinion has already been expressed by Mr. Zhu, the wording is even more painful than that of Mr. Zhu. Apart from accepting Mr. Sun's instructions with the utmost sincerity, we have nothing else to say. Here, on the one hand, we hope that all people who have suffered greatly but cannot eat their fill, or who are willing to endure hardship but have no hardship to endure, can have a thorough awakening and ask why most people suffer greatly but cannot eat their fill, or are willing to endure hardship but have no hardship to endure? Why do a few people not suffer at all and get [peace, wealth, and honor]? For our heavy responsibilities, we can all have a very clear understanding! At the same time, since Mr. Sun has such a clear understanding of our current serious problems, and is willing to discuss them with us in detail without being bothered, we hope that Mr. Sun will be able to provide us with more advice in the future.
