High School Curriculum Standards (2)

Physical Education 130

First, Objectives

(1) To continue physical training, so that physical and mental development is sound, in preparation for revitalizing the nation.

(2) To continue training civic morality through group sports.

(3) To cultivate the sports skills needed in life.

(4) To improve poor posture.

(5) To develop the habit of using sports as entertainment.

Second, Time Allocation

(1) Teaching time: two hours per week. (2) Morning exercises: ten minutes every morning. (3) Extracurricular sports: at least fifty minutes every day.

Third, Teaching Material Outline

(1) First School Year

(1) Games, (2) Group mixed continuous apparatus exercises, (3) Ball sports, (4) Track and field (reduced for girls), (5) National arts, (6) Dance (reduced for boys), (7) Natural activities, used as much as possible outside of class, (8) Corrective exercises, for those with physical defects, (9) Adopt the basic movements of ball sports, track and field, and apparatus exercises, and teach them in a natural way, (10) Gentle exercise (for those who should not engage in strenuous exercise).

(2) Second School Year

(1) Games, (2) Apparatus exercises, (3) Ball sports, (4) Track and field (reduced for girls), (5) National arts, (6) Dance (reduced for boys), (7) Swimming and skating, practice outside of class, (8) Corrective exercises, for those with physical defects, (9) Basic exercises, (10) Gentle exercise (for those who should not engage in strenuous exercise).

(3) Third School Year

(1) Apparatus exercises, (2) Ball games, (3) Track and field, (4) National arts, (5) Dance (reduced for boys), (6) Natural activities (including swimming, skating, climbing, riding, rowing, and others), used as much as possible outside of class, (7) Corrective exercises, for those with physical defects, (8) Group mixed continuous apparatus exercises, (9) Gentle exercise (for those who should not engage in strenuous exercise). (Note) If weather conditions prevent outdoor classes, physical education morality and sports rules can be lectured indoors.

Fourth, Summary of Implementation Methods

(1) Homework Items

(1) Regular class, (2) Morning exercises, (3) Extracurricular sports, (4) Organization of various extracurricular activities: 1. Intramural competitions, 2. Interscholastic competitions, 3. Outings and trips, 4. Various designs and performances.

(2) Teaching Method Key Points

Regarding high school physical education teaching methods, in addition to the principles of junior high school, attention should be paid to the training of leaders, in order to lead social sports after leaving school. The key points of the teaching method are listed below:

(1) Apply as much as possible all the learning methods and analytical learning methods of ordinary teaching methods, and the law of preparation, the law of exercise, and the law of effect of educational psychology.

(2) Regular class, morning exercises, and extracurricular sports should be mutually linked to avoid repetition, so as to avoid student fatigue.

1. In regular class, various sports focus on basic training and teaching of methods and rules. The teacher's work is heavier.

2. Extracurricular sports focus on students' actual practice. At this time, the teacher is only responsible for management.

3. Morning exercises or inter-class activities focus on gentle physical activities. Their role is to regulate life, and natural activities are the main focus.

(3) Use group competition methods as much as possible.

(4) Hold at least one skill test each semester. At the beginning of the semester, announce the test methods in advance to encourage students to practice hard at ordinary times.

(5) National arts should start with physical training, the posture should be correct, the movements should be lively, and the meaning and function of each movement should be clear.

(6) Schools without indoor physical education facilities should make full use of ordinary indoor facilities for special physical education activities.

(7) Sanitary facilities, such as bathrooms, should be fully provided.

(8) According to the environment of each school, formulate standards for skills, health, and common knowledge.

(9) Use holidays to create large group physical design activities, such as celebrations and joint sports meetings.

(10) Unite with other groups in sports to compare and promote progress.

(11) Conduct health examinations of all students three weeks after the start of each year.

(12) Use ability grouping methods as much as possible.

Physical education grading cannot be based on ordinary intelligence standards, because the ages of students in different regions are uneven, and the degree of physical development is different. Students of the same grade may not be suitable for the same type of teaching material. Therefore, within the possible range, ability grading methods should be used as much as possible. The grading methods should be based on the following six standards (see appendix).

Fifth, Appendix Grading Methods

(1) Gender, (2) Results of physical examination, (3) Age, height, weight, (4) Physical fitness, (5) Skills, (6) Grade level. The following is a brief explanation of these six grading methods:

(1) Gender After the ages of twelve and thirteen, the development of boys and girls gradually becomes different, and their interests also differ. Therefore, physical education in the ordinary science of high school should be completely separated into classes.

(2) Results of health examination Health examination is one of the most important events in school administration. At least one student should be examined once a year. The results of the examination should be used as a reference for physical education grading. Students with poor physical development or defects should be given special instruction.

(3) Age, height, weight It is extremely difficult to teach students of uneven ages and different development together in physical education class. Many schools use the age, height, and weight grading methods. Some use only one, some use two in combination, and some use all three in combination, and the combination of all three is the best. McCloy's Physical Ability Standards Score Table can be used. A simple method is attached below for application. It can still be changed when used. For example, the table is divided into seven grades. When applying it, it can be divided into two or three grades according to the index obtained by actual high school students.

A Sincere Appeal to National University and Middle School Students to Implement Education for National Salvation (10) by You Huai-gao 135

(10) The Only Method for National Construction [Corvée Labor]

After the implementation of educational construction, material construction is, of course, also extremely important. However, material construction requires a great deal of manpower. To expedite its realization within a few periods, it is necessary to implement universal corvée labor. Corvée labor should be divided into two types: military corvée labor and agricultural corvée labor.

Our country currently has more than two million soldiers, and uses 80% of the national income each year to support the troops. This is currently a major enemy that consumes national strength and hinders construction. I believe that the ancient-style national defense method of "raising troops for a thousand days to use them for one morning" is extremely uneconomical and that soldiers who are well-fed and have nothing to do are prone to misconduct. Rather than using the method of streamlining troops to reduce military expenditures, it is better to implement military corvée labor, which is relatively beneficial and easier to manage. In accordance with the policy of national construction, under the guidance of experts from the association, the military leaders of each province and region are responsible for completing the most important profit-generating projects and productive enterprises during this ten-year national salvation period. These include projects such as railways, highways, bridges, canals, dikes, and docks, as well as enterprises such as power generation, afforestation, mining, and heavy industry manufacturing. A small portion of the national army will be retained to undertake national defense, while the majority of the military will devote their efforts to construction. The results will be: (1) internal wars can be eliminated, (2) military expenditures can be reduced, (3) construction can be implemented, and (4) all soldiers in the country can fulfill some of their national salvation obligations.

The construction work of military corvée labor is a major undertaking that is tightly integrated, and it is a construction of a special kind of enterprise. It requires continuous work over ten years. The work of agricultural corvée labor is to be dispersed among the villages throughout the country, with farmers in each village taking on the affairs of their respective villages. Every year during the slack farming season in winter, agricultural corvée labor will be implemented under government orders, association guidance, and teacher supervision. The first phase is to organize village roads and open up village paths. The second phase is to open rivers, plant trees, relocate graves, and eliminate pests. The third phase is to construct public places and houses in the village. However, it is best to implement agricultural corvée labor two or three years after the implementation of educational labor, because by that time, the farmers throughout the country will have been enlightened and influenced by teachers, and at least will have gained some common knowledge as citizens. Or at least a portion of the farmers can be expected to participate voluntarily.

As for the grassroots organization of farmers, the county magistrates of each county throughout the country should be responsible, together with the district chiefs of each autonomous region, to jointly organize Education for National Salvation Advancement Associations in each village. Then, the government should issue an order, the gist of which is as follows:

[Within three months, the county magistrates of each county throughout the country should assist university and middle school students in organizing Education for National Salvation Associations in each county. Then, within six months, the county magistrates should convene the district chiefs of each autonomous region to organize Education for National Salvation Advancement Associations in each district to assist university and middle school students in establishing schools and encouraging farmers' children to attend school.]

(11) The Only Method for Defending the Nation [Military Service]

We can never abandon the fertile soil and the climate suitable for farming and animal husbandry that Heaven has given us. We can never abandon the vast land and numerous people that our ancestors have passed down to us. We can never allow Japan or any European or American country to become our master. We never want to kill people, but we will not allow others to kill us. We never want to seize other people's land, but we will not allow others to seize our land. We not only want to achieve equality between people, but also equality between countries. However, if we want to fulfill the above conditions, we cannot succeed without a great and well-organized military force. Therefore, we must implement military service in order to make the country independent and survive. However, the qualifications of the new soldiers of this 20th century must include education, scientific knowledge, military training, and moral cultivation. None of these four can be lacking. Therefore, I advocate that the period for implementing this military service should be at least five or six years after the implementation of educational service, because by that time, there will be at least millions of people who are qualified to become educated new soldiers, and tens of thousands of people who are qualified to become trained new military officers.

Therefore, our first step is national salvation, our second step is national construction, and our third step is national defense. Because the current military requires four elements: soldiers, generals, materials, and morale. In other words, it is a military that has undergone sufficient military training and is willing to give its life, generals and staff with overall talents who have experienced major battles, and leaders in various affairs, and the completeness of all kinds of combat equipment, military supplies, chemical materials, electrical appliances, and transportation facilities, and a great unified popular sentiment, which can be responsible for replenishing the military and materials. Therefore, in wartime, people can be seen diligently serving the public, and factories are manufacturing goods day and night. Therefore, the current scientific military movement requires at least ten years of full preparation from top to bottom, and it must be after production, manufacturing, education, and military administration are complete before it can deal with enemy countries that are scientifically advanced and have substantial military strength. Therefore, I extremely support the current government's policy of temporary submission to seek a way out, which is to preserve strength to seek final victory. This is why I advocate that military service should be implemented in five or six years. Because acting on emotions is useless.

As five people were reorganization personnel in the district, Mr. Kong Fanxi’s place of residence is in the jurisdiction of District Four. He has already been revoked by an order from the City Party Headquarters. Jiang Manqian has been separately appointed to fill the vacancy and serve as reorganization personnel in the district, it is said.

Since the Shanghai Library Association held its seventh annual meeting on December 18th, it has elected Du Dingyou, Kong Minzhong, and nine others as executive committee members. 暨南 Holds Southern Championship for Sixth Year 151

Yesterday's 2-2 Draw with Jiaotong University Means an Average of One More Point Keeps the Championship Ticket

—Auntie Wind Plays Tricks, Athletes from Both Teams Struggle to Show Their Strengths—

In recent years, the Southern University Football Championship has been a contest solely between Jinan and Jiaotong Universities. This year is no different. The final was held yesterday at Jinan University in Zhenru. At the time, there was no sun, and the north wind blew fiercely. Nearly a thousand spectators surrounded the field. In the end, the score was 2-2, a draw. Jinan University continued to hold the championship for the sixth year with one more point, truly worthy of being called lucky.

Jinan Holds for Six Years 152

The Southern University Football Tournament has now reached its seventh session. Jinan University has uniquely held it six times, no less than a fine tale in the history of football. And the changes in talent in the university football world can be roughly seen here. In the first session, Fudan showed great strength and dominated the South. In the second session, the football match was eventful, forming a triangle, with Jiaotong, Guanghua, and Jinan each occupying one side, sharing the championship equally. Since then, Jinan has seen frequent rises in talent, and its reputation has greatly increased. The only strong opponent is Jiaotong University. Therefore, the final has always been between the above two teams. In the third session, Jinan won 7-1; in the fourth, 2-1; in the fifth, 9-0; and in the sixth, 10-0. Jinan held the championship for five years. By the time of this seventh session, Jinan's famous players Chen Zhenhe, Jiang Shan Jing Zhuang, Shihong Mei Hongbao, and others were unable to play, and the combat strength was weakened. Jiaotong University, having been defeated repeatedly, had long resolved to avenge its humiliation. The opportunity to restore its glory suddenly came. Therefore, they put all their efforts into maneuvering. In yesterday's battle, each team won two goals, maintaining a draw. Jiaotong University ultimately lost the chance to fight again due to a 0-0 draw with Fudan in a previous match, resulting in an average of one less point. This year's championship belongs to Jinan again. Jiaotong University has not lost in this session, but in the end, it still returns with a runner-up title, which is also worth lamenting.

Referees Demand Protection 153

Since the assault case on referee Chen Jixiang, the Referee Association has generally refused all football matches within the scope of the Southern University. However, yesterday's Southern University final between Jiaotong and Jinan was still refereed by Jiang Xiangqing, a member of the association, which is puzzling. According to Mr. Jiang, the school authorities asked him to reluctantly do his best in a private capacity, and he will directly report to the Referee Association in the future and ask for punishment, and he is willing to donate all the referee transportation fees earned in one season as a fine. Furthermore, Mr. Jiang requested that both parties provide written safety guarantees before he would agree to enter the field to perform his duties to avoid accidental dangers. After the formalities were completed, the battle began, already fifteen minutes past the scheduled time.

The Great Battle Results in a Draw 154

Auntie Wind Teases the Balls. On the day of the great battle, Auntie Wind graced the scene, teasing the balls, making them unpredictable. The athletes from both teams were flustered. It is truly as they say, "Those who comply will live, and those who resist will die." Jinan took the lead with a score of 2-1 in the first half. Jiaotong also achieved a draw in the second half because of this. Moreover, balls that could often have been scored passed by the goal. What was unexpected turned into reality. This is all because Auntie Wind was playing tricks. No excellent passes or beautiful shots were seen, presumably also due to being trapped under the influence of Auntie Wind, unable to display their skills.

Li Chuanxin Wins the Lottery. The whistle blew, and the great battle began. Jinan attacked with the wind, relentlessly striking. Jiaotong's Zhang Ji Zeng and Chen Gongyu defended on the left and right, while Yang Yuhua, Zhang Jinrong, and Li Beiliang intercepted in the middle, causing Jinan's five forwards to be unable to enter. Suddenly, Luo Haiguang took a long shot. Fan Jiaju moved forward to receive it. Wang Nanzhen galloped to intercept. Fan kicked it out, hitting Wang's back, bouncing back towards the goal. The whole field was shocked. Unexpectedly, it was carried past the empty goal by Auntie Wind, rushing toward the direction. Jiaotong's goalie, He, praised it. The forwards immediately looked壮. Wan Xianghua took the lead, breaking through three barriers in a row. Shen Guanlan followed closely, passing the ball to the center. Xie, the goalkeeper, left his post to save the danger, leaving the goal wide open. Li Chuanxin arrived next, making a successful shot. Jiaotong opened the scoring first.

Wang Nanzhen Makes a Miraculous Contribution. Jinan's athletes, suffering this unexpected loss, were greatly enraged. The entire army devoted themselves, with no turning back. Liu Zukan's shot was missed by Fan, failing to pass through the gate. Zhang Hongzao lay down on the left side. When the time came, he quickly passed to the center. How strange! It repeatedly collided with Jiaotong's inner guard and the goalkeeper's legs, and finally bounced into the net from the goalpost, making it a draw. Jinan's momentum greatly increased, pressing relentlessly. Luo Haiguang shot towards the goal, hitting the post and bouncing back. During the struggle for possession, Wang Nanzhen, seeing that no one was prepared, secretly fired a cold arrow. Where the sound of the string started, it went deep into the net. Not long after, Jinan scored another goal, but it was ruled out due to Chen Zhenxiang's offside. At that time, the goalkeeper Fan was the target of public criticism, but he was able to defuse the danger, which was praised by the audience.

Shen Guanlan Sets the Draw. After the break, the war drums sounded again. Jiaotong turned from a disadvantage to taking advantage of the wind, and the atmosphere changed. Attacking was more common than defending. Jinan knew this and heavily guarded. As they held each other for five minutes, Wan Xianghua suddenly rose as a surprise soldier. Mai Tinglin was unable to stop him. Lai Zuorong rushed to help. Wan quickly passed to the center. At that time, the goalkeeper Xie was loyal and unwilling to submit, personally coming out to save the situation, leaving the goal empty. Shen Guanlan's leg rose, the ball went out, directly into the goal, again forming a 2-2 draw. At this critical moment, both sides worked hard and fought fiercely, forming a stalemate. After thirty minutes, Jinan got a free kick, the location was within the penalty area. Each side arranged their formations, competing with each other's intelligence. In the end, it was ineffective. Until the sound of the retreat signal, it was still a 2-2 draw. In total, in each game, Jinan had one more point (9 compared to 8), maintaining the sixth-year championship.

Free Talk

A Murder on the Winter Solstice Morning 158

— Lin Yutang

Confucius said that the upper class kills with the pen, the middle class kills with words, and the lower class kills with stone slabs. It can be seen that there are many ways to kill. I just met a guest, and because he was too good at talking, I killed him with two and a half sentences. Although whether he lives or dies is up to him, whether I kill him is up to me, fulfilling my duty as a middle class person.

The matter is like this. Although I don't believe in Jesus, I observe Christmas, which is commonly known as the foreign Winter Solstice. In the past few days, because Christmas is coming, I have been extra busy, buying things I shouldn't buy, playing with the children more, and during this festive season, I seem to feel that I should be particularly lazy. Therefore, the manuscript for the China Critic [Small Critic] has not been written. The person who collects the manuscript wants it within twenty minutes. Originally, I am very systematic in handling affairs, but at this time, I want to be unsystematic for once. I think that if a person does things properly all year round, it's nothing to mess up during this festive season, right? Even if the China Critic cannot be published on schedule, China will not perish because of it, right? So, I am sitting by an iron stove, dreaming of the pleasure of watching the fire in a fireplace, temporarily putting all the worries in my heart into the dream fire, turning them into nothing, and flying up to the blue sky. Only because I am naturally well-behaved, even though I am sitting and dreaming, I still glance at that typewriter from time to time. As a result, I understand the big picture, and my desire to be lazy is overcome. I make up my mind and am preparing to work.

Just as I was rushing to write the manuscript, knowing that there was an article to write, but not knowing how to start, the doorbell suddenly rang. Looking at the card, it was a stranger. This made me embarrassed, because if it was a familiar guest, I could wish him a Merry Christmas and then ask him to get lost. However, the situation of the visitor seemed very important. So, I asked the servant to tell the visitor first that I was very busy at the moment, but if there was anything important, he could come in and sit and talk for a few minutes. He said that the matter was very urgent. So, he came in.

This gentleman was very well-dressed and behaved very elegantly. In fact, looking at his name card printed in a Song Dynasty style, one would know that he was a member of the academic community. His forehead was very high, very much like a literary scholar. But his mouth was pointed and small, and his eyes were narrow, which didn't make people like him very much. He was holding a paper bag in his hand. I was already ill-disposed towards him.

So, we began to exchange greetings. Mr. So-and-so had long admired my [great name] and had also read my [great works].

[Very shallow. Please don't laugh, sir.] I replied respectfully as usual. But as soon as these words came out, I immediately felt bad. I had a feeling that we would have to pay our respects to each other for another fifteen minutes, going around in circles, before there was any hope of getting to the point. I didn't know what his business was after all.

To be honest, I have a lot of experience in receiving guests. Generally, the more knowledgeable and polite the visitor is, the more greetings and roundabout words there are. Everyone knows that it is not good to be impolite when meeting a stranger, like a foreigner saying "I'm here for such and such a matter" and opening the topic directly, because this way of opening the topic is not elegant. When scholars meet for the first time, they must have the identity of a scholar, taking out the effort of writing eight-legged essays or the righteous method of the Tongcheng School. When talking like this, it is called having articles in the words. Articles should not only have style but also have structure. It can probably be divided into four paragraphs. However, talking is not like writing an article, starting with breaking the topic and carrying on the topic; the words to enter the topic should be left to the end. These four paragraphs are like this: (1) talk about greetings, comment on the climate, (2) describe the past, pursue old friendships, (3) talk about current affairs, express emotions, (4) the [small matter] to be entrusted. No scholar is willing to start from the fourth paragraph. They must use the chapters, with foreshadowing, carrying on, and the momentum is strong, and then suddenly stop, stopping abruptly under the virtue of reality. If these four paragraphs are classified using the book classification method, they can also be divided into (1) meteorology, (2) history, (3) politics, (4) economics. The role of the first paragraph is to [sit in hiding], in line with the meaning of "when they come, be at peace with them." [Your surname] [your given name] [I have long admired you] [I have long been away from you] and [the weather today haha] belong to this paragraph. Only when the position is secure can the feelings be settled. The so-called settling feelings does not refer to the evening of settling feelings but is only for connecting feelings. Therefore, the second paragraph is about describing the old. Maybe your nephew went to school with Mr. So-and-so, maybe you lived on South Small Street, and he lived in No Amount of Adult Hutong. Thus, feelings are blended together. If everyone is from Peking University, knows Zhimo, Shizhi, or even Gu Hongming, Lin Qin'nan..., then it will be even more intimate and talkative. When feelings are good and the momentum is strong, the next step is to talk about current affairs and express emotions. This third paragraph has a wide range, including: it is unreasonable for China not to perish, national salvation policies, and comments on the political leaders of Guyue Sanwang Caojiang Ma Er Gongchang, and so on. There are also statistics on following President Sun for how many years. For example, if you heard President Sun give a speech once in the thirty-first year of Guangxu, and this year is the twenty-first year of the Republic of China, the total should be twenty-five years. This is called following President Sun for twenty-five years. When feelings are good and the momentum is strong, the time to start suddenly has come. So, the guest drinks tea and stands up, picks up his hat, and suddenly turns into the fourth paragraph: There is a small matter to ask of you now. Sir, do you know the principal of ○○ University? Could you please write a letter of introduction? Summarize the whole article.

On this Winter Solstice morning, my nerves are sensitive, and I know that I am going to listen to an article with the four-paragraph method again. Because Mr. So-and-so's speech is very elegant and his behavior is very dignified, I am a little prepared. In my heart, I am guessing what treasures are in his paper bag. Or is he going to introduce me to some errand? Even so, we still start with meteorology.

The zodiac signs have been calculated, and Mr. So-and-so casually mentions Fu Junlai. Fu Junlai is a top student at Peking University. I understand that he is describing the old, already in the second paragraph. Yes, this gentleman is indeed talented, with a light of ten thousand feet in his chest and a very strong pen. I completely agree, but my eyes always shoot back on the typewriter and his paper bag. However, without knowing it, our feelings have indeed blended together. What this gentleman talks about is reasonable and pertinent.

The transition from the second paragraph to the third paragraph is very natural.

Fu Jun, a native of Shu. You see, isn't there a fratricidal killing in Sichuan? Mr. So-and-so said Sichuan is very unfortunate. He said he saw the Analects Biweekly (I heard people say they saw the Analects Biweekly. I'm always happy.) and knew that there had been four hundred and seventy-seven civil wars in Sichuan since the Republic of China. I naturally have no objection, but I think in my heart: [Chinese people have too much time.] The China Critic's servant is coming to pick up the manuscript, so I am not willing to listen to his arguments anymore, appreciate his chapters, but am very willing to help him end the third paragraph. We have been talking for more than half an hour. At this time, I feel that it wouldn't hurt to hang all the Sichuan warlords and move on to the main topic.

[Sir, what is your business in visiting today?]

[Just a small matter,] he said, opening his paper bag. [I heard that you and Mr. Hu, the editor of a certain magazine, are relatives. Could I trouble you to forward this manuscript to Mr. Hu?]

[Mr. Hu and I are not relatives, and I have never heard of the name of that magazine,] I replied wildly against my will, feeling that I had the outline of a middle-class person killing someone. At this time, the plot is very tense. Because of this sudden attack, not only was it beyond my own expectations, but even this gentleman was stunned. We both felt dumbfounded, because we deeply regretted that such a good article, which took half a point to do the groundwork and just wanted to enter the topic, was made to have no ending because of my madness. My sin is really no less than that of who kicked over the seven-star lamp. At this time, we both felt that life is like a dream! Because I know that I have wasted my most precious Winter Solstice morning in vain, and he also feels that he has wasted his knowledge of meteorology, astronomy, history, and politics in vain.

New Year's Office Closure for Three Days 159

— Ye Shengtao

The three-day New Year's office closure has been approved, and it is also said that "a notice is sent to the whole country to handle it uniformly." All service gentlemen are certain to have three days of "playing around."

Some time ago, it was reported in the newspaper that all New Year celebrations and other activities would be免除ed, the reason being that we are still in a time of national crisis. It seems that there was also a proposal to continue working as usual during the New Year. If you ask why, even a primary school student can answer, nothing more than "national crisis is pressing" and "work is tight." This is consistent with the practice of eating vegetarian food for one day on National Humiliation Day, which, in short, is [lying on firewood and tasting gall].

Suffering hardships, facing each other with sad faces, is the norm of human nature. However, a sad face must coexist with resolute implementation and sincere hope to have meaning. If there is nothing else besides a sad face, then you can only be sad for the rest of your life. Even if you are sad to death, who will pay attention to you?

Speaking of work, it is usually said that progress is good, and stagnation is not good. For example, a carpenter, if he stops working for a day, he will make two fewer chairs. If he doesn't stop, he will make two more chairs. Work stagnation reduces efficiency, so it is not good. However, it cannot be generalized. Some work has almost no efficiency. It is always in progress there. There is nothing good about it. Even if it stagnates for a lifetime, there is nothing wrong with it. Let's take an example, the so-called [office work] of [waiting for instructions and then following them] is such.

Recently, I read Wang Yinchuan's [A History of the Successful Struggle of the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan]. The book records what a middle-aged woman said to the author: [In the past, although our lives were comfortable, it was only for our minority. The majority of people were much worse than our current situation. Now, although our minority is not as good as before, the majority of people are better than before. This is also how justice should be....

What's more, government personnel sell our saved materials to foreign countries, exchange them for cash, buy machinery, and build these many factories, railways, houses, etc. We can see it with our own eyes. Although our current life is not very satisfactory, although it is difficult, we have hope. It is not very satisfactory, but it is rich in difficulty, and the whole country has the same unsatisfactory and difficulty.]

×　　×　　×　　×　　×

When saying this, that woman was probably also showing a sad face. Think about it, what kind of strength and heart coexist with her sad face? The five-year plan was completed in four years, which is the overall expression of efficiency. In such a huge project, of course, no one can be lazy. If there is nothing else besides a sad face, it is better to pursue joy and seek laughter. This is ultimately beneficial to health. Anyway, progress and stagnation are like two fives and ten, what does it matter if you stop for a while? Therefore, the method of issuing a notice to the whole country to stop working for three days during the New Year is worthy of our praise.

×　　×　　×　　×　　×

［There is No Moon on New Year's Eve Every Year］ 160

— Yang Xingzhi

I have been away from my hometown for five years. The customs of greeting, kowtowing, and saying auspicious words to celebrate New Year's Day in my hometown have long been increasingly blurred in my memory. Only the saying [There is no moon on New Year's Eve every year] is still deeply engraved in my mind, and the more I think about it, the more I learn that it is [very meaningful.]

Originally, it is indeed a disappointing thing that there is no moon on New Year's Eve. If it is [New Year's Eve] and [there is a moon], then when people [gather with their families and drink to their heart's content], looking up at the bright moon in the sky, everyone bathing in the silver [light], there is no need to set off firecrackers to break the silence, nor is there a need to hold torches to illuminate the darkness. This can even make people add some [joy] to the [happiness]! However, in my experience, the past twenty-seven New Year's Eves have all been without a moon, and each time it has been a dark, deathly night.

Probably because everyone is unwilling to have no moon on New Year's Eve, a [revolution] was launched vigorously not long ago. This revolution 革ed the [lunar calendar] to use the [solar calendar], dragging New Year's Eve out from under the fate of the [obscure] character. The revolution then [succeeded], and everyone was happy, thinking that from now on there would be a moon on New Year's Eve, even if there was no bright moon, at least it should not be [pitch black.] But hope finally deceived us. This year's New Year's Eve is still as [dark] as in previous years, and the darkness is mixed with rain, making people shiver!

I don't remember which British or American person said this: [Since 1929, we have never had a Merry Christmas], but, God knows, we are even worse. Since we were born, we have never had a New Year's Eve with a moon!

Let's get to work and transform this dark world. This way, maybe we can finally have a [New Year's Eve with a moon]!

Mr. Lao She's Letter Says: 161

Mr. Liewen:

You asked me for short essays; to be honest, I'm not good at them. Please look this way. I have a private matter to say: I'm skilled at both grand and medium-sized writings -- it seems unnecessary to say the latter part. If you don't believe me, ask Aunt Ma; am I not a literary master of grand writings? However, you insist on making things difficult for me, and I have my own ideas. You see, I only need to slide down from the grand style to become a medium style; then slide down from the medium style to become a short style, perhaps that will work? But, from the perspective of Chinese literary history, grand writings are truly rare and precious (a phoenix with horns is a type of amphibious animal, it is said). In our [National Writings] -- this should be listed alongside National Arts, National Shame, and National Studies, not the document held by the ambassador to England or France -- I have never seen a single grand poem or essay. Perhaps you believe this? For this reason, I am somewhat indifferent to short essays after all: you see, I want to add a few grand works to the National Writings. I must aim for the highest of the high, in order to attain the high; I must run to the top of the limitless, so as to generate the Tai Chi. Tai Chi Chuan is a National Art, and Tai Chi writing would be perfect as National Writings. When my masterpiece is born, even George Bernard Shaw and William Shakespeare will have to acquire Chinese nationality and learn our National Studies. Therefore, I still cannot slide downwards; "carp leaping over the dragon gate" is my attitude. Do you know the grand method of grand writing? Have you seen God create man? I know, I have seen it. God said, "Let there be light in the world," and with a swoosh! Golden light radiated everywhere, fifteen suns, along with hundreds of millions of stars of various sizes, all laughing together. God said, "Let there be people in the world," with a bang! A sea of people, human hearts and lungs, human feelings and reason, human lives hanging in the balance. You see, my grand method of grand writing, even if it is incompetent, must resemble this. You ask me to write short essays, if I lack even a bit of humor, it would be extremely anxious and unacceptable!

If you think this is all wrong, then what exactly is a short essay in your opinion! Wishing you

good luck! Your younger brother Lao She, bowing

December 28th, Jinan

>Long Novel

The Age of P and the Crossroads of Love, Part 32 162

— Zhang Ziping

They were both shelling melon seeds. A silence settled between them for a while. Haiquan suddenly thought of Mrs. Tsuruko at this moment. At the same time, he suspected what Ms. Zhuo had called him here for. He wanted to ask her directly, but he hesitated politely.

[I originally disliked this place. But there was no other way; I couldn't find a suitable house for a while. You see, two or three families live in this one house.]

[What kind of family lives downstairs?]

Haiquan asked this directly. She didn't answer immediately; he saw her cheeks turn slightly red.

[We sublet from downstairs. After moving in, we learned that they were...]

She said, her cheeks reddening even more, and she lowered her head.

[Then you should move sooner.]

[Haven't I already told my mother? But… Mr. Lin, you're not an outsider; to be honest with you, we really can't afford a too expensive house. I have an older brother who works as a small clerk in the ×× Bureau, and his monthly salary is only thirty-odd dollars. When my father wasn't dead…]

She was complaining in this way, as if feeling endless emotions.

[How many siblings do you have?]

[One older brother, one older sister, and I am the youngest.]

[What about your sister?]

When Haiquan asked this, she hesitated again. After a while, she said,

[Married and went to Tianjin with her husband.]

After sitting for a while longer, a maid brought him a cup of lukewarm, brown tea. Haiquan felt a bit embarrassed sitting there and wanted to take his leave. But Zhuo Shuhua noticed.

[Let me go call my mother and brother to meet you. They really want to get to know you.]

She said as she walked out. She didn't seem to go downstairs. He thought, she probably went to the attic. In just a moment, she walked back smiling. She dragged a chair and sat closer to him. He smelled an intriguing fragrance.

[It wouldn't be bad to put my arm around her and smell the fragrance. At most, she'll laugh and scold me and walk away. If I had the courage, I might not even hit a wall.]

But he was only thinking it; his face was already flushed red. At the same time, he was afraid that this base behavior would cause her to despise him.

[What does it matter if she despises me? The truth is, I completely lack any courage.]

[Mr. Lin, I heard that your brother-in-law is a high-ranking official in the Ministry of Finance, is that true?]

[That's not true.]

He quickly denied it. But he already sensed that she was asking about that Master Ren.

[That's what everyone says, his surname is Yin.]

She tilted her head, looking thoughtful.
